add_namespace = newengland

### Creating New England
country_event = { # Occupy New England
	id = newengland.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.1"}
	title = newengland.1.t
	desc = newengland.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = newengland.1.a
		ai_chance = { # Take New England
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_TAKE
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = USA
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					tag = USA
					tag = CSA
					tag = TEX
					tag = CAL
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				remove_unit_leader = 86
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_TAKE
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
}

country_event = { # ACW nation informed that Canada has seized New England
	id = newengland.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.2"}
	title = newengland.2.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots
	
	desc = {
		text = newengland.2.d
		trigger = { country_exists = CSA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.2.d.nocsa
		trigger = { NOT = { country_exists = CSA } }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = occupied_new_england
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # This means War!
		name = newengland.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = USA
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
					NOT = { country_exists = TEX }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = TEX
					tag = CAL
				}
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CAN
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = { # Next time Canada!
		name = newengland.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada doesn't occupy New England
	id = newengland.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.3"}
	title = newengland.3.t
	desc = newengland.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		country_exists = CSA
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.3.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_new_england_units
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = USA_civil_war_newengland
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada Releases New England
	id = newengland.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.5"}
	title = newengland.5.t
	desc = newengland.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		is_subject = no
		is_faction_leader = yes
		932 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
			} #Massachusetts
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = CSA
			country_exists = NEE
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_new_england
						option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_CAN_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_WASHINGTON_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_KENNEDY_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_ASTOR_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_MILITARY_COUP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_LOVECRAFT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			NEE = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = NEE
		add_to_faction = NEE
		set_country_flag = CAN_new_england_decision
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				NEE = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "La Resistance"	}
				NEE = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Virginia Hall"
						GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_virginia_hall
						traits = { operative_demolition_expert }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						female = yes
						nationalities = { NEE USA }
					}
				}
			}
			NEE = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.6
					days = 2
				}
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.101
					days = 9
				}
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.2009
					days = 30
				}
				load_oob = NEE
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }

                set_popularities = {
                    totalist = 0
                    radical_socialist = 0
                    syndicalist = 0
                    social_democrat = 4
                    social_liberal = 28
                    market_liberal = 32
                    social_conservative = 36
                    authoritarian_democrat = 0
                    paternal_autocrat = 0
                    national_populist = 0
                }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.5.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			NEE = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = NEE
		add_to_faction = NEE
		set_country_flag = CAN_new_england_decision
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				NEE = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "La Resistance"	}
				NEE = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Virginia Hall"
						GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_virginia_hall
						traits = { operative_demolition_expert }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						female = yes
						nationalities = { NEE USA }
					}
				}
			}
			NEE = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.6
					days = 2
				}
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.101
					days = 9
				}
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.2009
					days = 30
				}
				load_oob = NEE
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }

                set_popularities = {
                    totalist = 0
                    radical_socialist = 0
                    syndicalist = 0
                    social_democrat = 4
                    social_liberal = 28
                    market_liberal = 32
                    social_conservative = 36
                    authoritarian_democrat = 0
                    paternal_autocrat = 0
                    national_populist = 0
                }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			change_tag_from = CAN
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.5.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_new_england
						option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		set_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_state
		set_country_flag = CAN_new_england_decision
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				CAN_yankee_rebellion = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "La Resistance"	}
				CAN = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Virginia Hall"
						GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_virginia_hall
						traits = { operative_demolition_expert }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						female = yes
						nationalities = { CAN USA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Independent New England
	id = newengland.6
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.6"}
	title = newengland.6.t
	desc = newengland.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = newengland.6.a
		add_political_power = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.41
				days = 122
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.44
				days = 162
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.54
				days = 200
				random = 100
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.64
				days = 400
				random = 1000
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.59
				days = 600
				random = 3000
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # America is reunited
	id = newengland.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.7"}
	title = newengland.7.t
	desc = newengland.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		owns_state = 361 #Maryland
		owns_state = 371 #Louisiana
		owns_state = 395 #Illinois
		owns_state = 797 #San Francisco
		owns_state = 932 #Massachusetts
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_united_america
			country_exists = TEX
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = CAL
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "H.P. Lovecraft" ruling_only = yes } }
		}
		name = newengland.7.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_claimed_america
		set_country_flag = NEE_united_america
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_template = "Resistance"
				check_variable = {
					created_resistance_template = 1
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Resistance"
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_ACW_cores = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "H.P. Lovecraft" ruling_only = yes }
		}
		name = newengland.7.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_claimed_america
		set_country_flag = NEE_united_america
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america_lovecraft
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_template = "Resistance"
				check_variable = {
					created_resistance_template = 1
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Resistance"
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_ACW_cores = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = newengland.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.10"}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # don't Pass the Act
		name = newengland.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_ideas = NEE_labor_relations1
		add_political_power = -80
	}
	option = { # don't Pass the Act
		name = newengland.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_political_power = 80
	}
}

country_event = { # New England requests home rule
	id = newengland.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.12"}
	title = newengland.12.t
	desc = newengland.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NEE = {
			is_subject_of = CAN
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.12.a #give them home rule
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = NEE
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.13
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.12.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		NEE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = ITA_outraged
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.14
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England granted home rule
	id = newengland.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.13"}
	title = newengland.13.t
	desc = newengland.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject_of = CAN
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.13.a
		add_political_power = 50
		overlord = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = NEE
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_legitimacy_plus_5_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			var = NEE_legitimacy
			value = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England refused home rule
	id = newengland.14
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.14"}
	title = newengland.14.t
	desc = newengland.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject_of = CAN
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.14.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_refused_home_rule
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_legitimacy_minus_10_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			var = NEE_legitimacy
			value = -10
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			 modifier = {
                factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_CAN_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_WASHINGTON_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_MILITARY_COUP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_LOVECRAFT
					}
				}
            }
		}
		name = newengland.14.b
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.238 days = 9 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Declaration of Independence
	id = newengland.15
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.15"}
	title = newengland.15.t
	desc = { # Normal Declaration
		text = newengland.15.d
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}
	desc = { # Leftist Declaration
		text = newengland.15.d.leftist
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = newengland.15.a #We're fine with it
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		add_political_power = -100
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.15.b #How dare they!
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_elected_government = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = NEE
						ratio < 1.0
					}
				}

			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.05
		declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = FROM
		}
	}
}


### Elections
country_event = { # The Provisional Government
	id = newengland.20
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.20"}
	title = newengland.20.t
	desc = newengland.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {# William Averell Harriman
				name = "William Averell Harriman"
				desc = "POLITICS_WILLIAM_HARRIMAN_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_NEE_william_harriman.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
				traits = {
					financial_expert
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {# Percival P. Baxter
				name = "Percival P. Baxter"
				desc = "POLITICS_PERCIVAL_BAXTER_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_NEE_Percival_P_Baxter.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = market_liberal_subtype
				traits = {
					nationalist_symbol
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {# Curley
				name = "James Michael Curley"
				desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_MICHAEL_CURLEY_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Jim_Curley.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				traits = {
					political_boss
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # George Aiken
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = radicals_in_power
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_REPUBLICAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_LIBERAL_REPUBLICAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_DEMOCRAT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = newengland.20.a
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = NEE_George_Aiken_hog_sde
			add_ideas = NEE_Frederick_Hale_for_sde
			add_ideas = NEE_Scott_Nearing_eco_sde
			add_ideas = NEE_Edith_Nourse_Rogers_sec_sde
		}
		create_country_leader = {
					name = "George Aiken"
					desc = "POLITICS_GEORGE_AIKEN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/George_Aiken.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						captain_of_industry
		}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = NEE_social_democrat_party_NP
			long_name = NEE_social_democrat_party_long_NP
			ideology = social_democrat
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # William Averell Harriman
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = radicals_in_power
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_NATIONAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_REPUBLICAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_DEMOCRAT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = newengland.20.b
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = NEE_John_Gilbert_Winant_hog_sli
			add_ideas = NEE_George_Higgins_Moses_for_sli
			add_ideas = NEE_Charles_Russell_Clason_eco_sli
			add_ideas = NEE_Wallace_Humphrey_White_Jr_sec_sli
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Percival P. Baxter
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = radicals_in_power
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

### 1940 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1940 National Party Primary
	id = newengland.21
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.21"}
	title = newengland.21.t
	desc = newengland.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # George Aiken
		name = newengland.21.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1940_liberal_primary_aiken
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = newengland.22
			days = 4
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Frances Perkins
		name = newengland.21.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1940_liberal_primary_perkins
			
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = newengland.22
			days = 4
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Election
	id = newengland.24
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.24"}
	title = newengland.24.t
	desc = newengland.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
	has_country_flag = NEE_election_time
	NOT = { 
		OR = {
			has_government = paternal_autocrat 
			has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			if = { # Joseph Kennedy Sr.
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1940_democratic_primary_kennedy
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Joseph Kennedy Sr."
					desc = "POLITICS_JOSEPH_KENNEDY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_joseph_kennedy_sr.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { tenacious_negotiator }
				}
			}

			else_if = { # James Curley
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1940_democratic_primary_curley
				}
				create_country_leader = {# Curley
					name = "James Michael Curley"
					desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_MICHAEL_CURLEY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Jim_Curley.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						political_boss
					}
				}
			}

			if = { # Al Smith
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1940_democratic_primary_smith
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Al Smith"
					desc = "POLITICS_AL_SMITH_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Al_Smith.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { political_boss }
				}
			}
			
			if = { # John Gilbert Winant
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1940_liberal_republican_primary_winant
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Gilbert Winant"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_WINANT_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_john_winant.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						tenacious_negotiator
					}
				}
			}
			
			else_if = { # Herbert H. Lehman
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1940_liberal_republican_primary_lehman
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = " Herbert H. Lehman"
					desc = "POLITICS_HERBERT_LEHMAN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_Robert_Lehman.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						financial_expert
					}
				}
			}
			
			else_if = { # Hamilton Fish
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1940_republican_primary_fish
				}
				create_country_leader = {# Fish
					name = "Hamilton Fish III"
					desc = "POLITICS_HAMILTON_FISH_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_hamilton_fish_iii.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						hog_reformist_soldier
					}
				}
			}
			
			else_if = { # Percival P. Baxter
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1940_republican_primary_baxter
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Percival P. Baxter"
					desc = "POLITICS_PERCIVAL_BAXTER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_Percival_P_Baxter.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"

### 1944 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1944 National Party Primary
	id = newengland.2525
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.25"}
	title = newengland.2525.t
	desc = { # National Party has the Presidency
		text = newengland.2525.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # National Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.2525.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		date > 1944.6.10
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		}
		NOT = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Frances Perkins
		name = newengland.2525.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_primary_perkins
		}
	}
	option = { # Ernest W. Gibson
		name = newengland.2525.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_primary_gibson
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.2525.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 election
	id = newengland.28
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.28"}
	title = newengland.28.t
	desc = newengland.28.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			if = { # Frances Perkins
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_primary_perkins

						economic_reformer
					}

			}

				limit = {

				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Ernest W. Gibson"
					desc = "POLITICS_ERNEST_GIBSON_DESC"
					picture = "Ernest_William_Gibson_Jr.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { economic_reformer }
				}
			}
			if = { # Dennis J. Roberts
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_republican_primary_roberts
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Dennis J. Roberts "
					desc = "POLITICS_DENNIS_ROBERTS_DESC"

				add_ideas = NEE_Charles_Russell_Clason_eco_sli
				add_ideas = NEE_Wallace_Humphrey_White_Jr_sec_sli
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = newengland.61
						days = 50
						random = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Republican
		name = newengland.28.c
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_election_republican
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Sherman Adams
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_republican_primary_adams
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_Sherman_Adams_hog_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_John_Hay_Whitney_for_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Harry_Gabriel_Hamlet_eco_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Pierrepont_Burt_Noyes_sec_mli
			}
			else_if = { # Robert F. Bradford
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_republican_primary_bradford
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_Robert_F_Bradford_hog_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_John_Hay_Whitney_for_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Harry_Gabriel_Hamlet_eco_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Pierrepont_Burt_Noyes_sec_mli
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = newengland.28.e
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_election_democrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Christian Herter
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_democratic_primary_herter
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_Christian_Herter_hog_sco
				add_ideas = NEE_Dean_Gooderham_Acheson_for_sco
				add_ideas = NEE_William_Stuart_Symington_Jr_eco_sco
				add_ideas = NEE_Wilbur_Lucius_Cross_sec_sco
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Quaker
		name = newengland.24.f
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1940_election_quaker
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			NEE_Eleanor_Roosevelt_hog_rso
			NEE_Whittaker_Chambers_for_rso
			NEE_Lillian_Willoughby_eco_rso
			NEE_Emily_Greene_Balch_sec_rso
		}
	}

### 1948 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1948 Liberal Primary
	id = newengland.29
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.29"}
	title = newengland.29.t
	desc = { # Liberal Party won the presidency just last time
		text = newengland.29.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = NEE_1940_election_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Liberal Party won also in 1940
		text = newengland.29.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_country_flag = NEE_1940_election_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Liberal Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.29.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		date > 1948.6.10
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		}
		NOT = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Maurice J. Tobin
		name = newengland.29.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = NEE_1940_election_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_tobin
		}
	}
	option = { # Paul A. Dever
		name = newengland.29.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = NEE_1940_election_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_dever
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.29.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = NEE_1940_election_liberal
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1948 election
	id = newengland.32
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.32"}
	title = newengland.32.t
	desc = newengland.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			if = { # Maurice J. Tobin
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_tobin
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Maurice J. Tobin"
					desc = "POLITICS_MAURICE_TOBIN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_Maurice_Tobin.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { divided_interests }
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Paul A. Dever
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_dever
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Paul A. Dever"
					desc = "POLITICS_PAUL_DEVER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_Paul_A_Dever.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { armaments_organizer }
				}
			}
			if = { # George Aiken
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_republican_primary_aiken
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "George Aiken"
					desc = "POLITICS_GEORGE_AIKEN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/George_Aiken.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { captain_of_industry }
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Robert F. Bradford
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_republican_primary_bradford
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Robert F. Bradford"
					desc = "POLITICS_ROBERT_BRADFORD_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_Robert_Bradford.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { economist }
				}
			}
			if = { # Thomas C. Hart
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1948_democratic_primary_hickenlooper
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Thomas C. Hart"
					desc = "POLITICS_THOMAS_HART_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_NEE_Thomas_Hart.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { quartermaster_general }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Liberal
		name = newengland.32.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_election_liberal
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Maurice J. Tobin
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_tobin
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_Maurice_J_Tobin_hog_sli
				add_ideas = NEE_Henry_Styles_Bridges_for_sli
				add_ideas = NEE_Ralph_Edward_Flanders_eco_sli
				add_ideas = NEE_Edith_Nourse_Rogers_sec_sde
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = newengland.62
						days = 50
						random = 100
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Paul A. Dever
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_dever
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_Paul_A_Dever_hog_sli
				add_ideas = NEE_Henry_Styles_Bridges_for_sli
				add_ideas = NEE_Ralph_Edward_Flanders_eco_sli
				add_ideas = NEE_Edith_Nourse_Rogers_sec_sde
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Republican
		name = newengland.32.b
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_election_republican
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # George Aiken
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_republican_primary_aiken
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_George_Aiken_hog_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Robert_Helyer_Thayer_for_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Leslie_Richard_Groves_Jr_eco_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Warren_Fales_Draper_sec_mli
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Robert F. Bradford
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_republican_primary_bradford
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_Robert_F_Bradford_hog_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Robert_Helyer_Thayer_for_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Leslie_Richard_Groves_Jr_eco_mli
				add_ideas = NEE_Warren_Fales_Draper_sec_mli
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = newengland.32.c
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_election_democrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Thomas C. Hart
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1948_democratic_primary_hickenlooper
				}
				add_ideas = NEE_Thomas_C_Hart_hog_sco
				add_ideas = NEE_James_Aloysius_'Jim'_Farley_for_sco
				add_ideas = NEE_Edward_Carleton_Moran_Jr_eco_sco
				add_ideas = NEE_James_Andrew_Shanley_sec_sco
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Quaker
		name = newengland.24.f
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1940_election_quaker
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.20
		}

			election_frequency = 48

		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			NEE_Eleanor_Roosevelt_hog_rso
			NEE_Whittaker_Chambers_for_rso
			NEE_Lillian_Willoughby_eco_rso
			NEE_Emily_Greene_Balch_sec_rso
		}
	}

### 1952 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1952 Liberal Primary
	id = newengland.34
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.34"}
	title = newengland.34.t
	desc = { # Liberal Party won the presidency just last time
		text = newengland.34.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = NEE_1944_election_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Liberal Party won also in 1944
		text = newengland.34.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_country_flag = NEE_1944_election_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Liberal Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.34.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		date > 1952.6.10
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1952_election
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Paul A. Dever
		name = newengland.34.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = NEE_1944_election_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_progressive_primary_dever
		}
	}
	option = { # Charles Poletti
		name = newengland.34.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = NEE_1944_election_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_progressive_primary_poletti
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.34.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = NEE_1944_election_liberal
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Successful Smuggling action in the Great Lakes Region (Underground Railroad)
	id = newengland.52
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.52"}
	title = newengland.52.t
	desc = newengland.52.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_new_england_great_migration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = CSA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CSA
		}
		NOT = {
		has_socialist_government = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			multiply_variable = {
				var = NEE_ugr_csa_manpower
				value = 1.1
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = NEE_ugr_csa_guns
				value = 1.1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # The Resistance grows Stronger!
		name = newengland.52.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_ugr_csa_10p_increase
		add_manpower = 13789
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 756
			producer = CSA
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = artillery_equipment_1
			amount = 23
			producer = CSA
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_white_line
		random_list = {
			66 = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.52
					days = 25
					random = 168
				}
			}
			34 = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.53
					days = 8
					random = 144
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
}

	desc = newengland.58.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = TEX
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = TEX
		}
		TEX = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.56
				days = 35
				random = 72
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Impose Quotas
		name = newengland.58.a
		multiply_variable = {
			var = NEE_ugr_tex_manpower
			value = 0.5
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}

	option = { # We are their only hope
		name = newengland.58.b
		multiply_variable = {
			var = NEE_ugr_tex_manpower
			value = 2
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = NEE_ugr_tex_times
			value = -5
		}
		add_manpower = 10000
		add_stability = -0.15
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.59"}
	title = newengland.59.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.59_lovecraft
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "H.P. Lovecraft"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.59.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "H.P. Lovecraft"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
		
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Robert Frost, Modernist Master
		name = newengland.59.a
		add_political_power = 20
	}
	option = { # H.P Lovecraft, the master of horror
		name = newengland.59.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
}

### Rebellion Events
country_event = { # The Yankee Rebellion
	id = newengland.80
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.80"}
	title = newengland.80.t
	desc = newengland.80.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		OR = {
			357 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Maine
			934 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #New Hampshire
			933 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Vermont
			932 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Massachusetts
			935 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Rhode Island
			931 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Connecticut
			796 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Upstate New York
		}
		has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_state
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
			country_exists = NEE
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_new_england
						option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			set_state_flag = CAN_in_rebellion
			hidden_effect = {
				ROOT = {
					add_to_variable = {
						var = CAN_yankee_rebellion
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.80.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			NEE = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = NEE
		add_to_faction = NEE
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				NEE = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			NEE = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.6
					days = 2
				}
				load_oob = NEE
			}
			NEE = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Virginia Hall"
						GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_virginia_hall
						traits = { operative_demolition_expert }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						female = yes
						nationalities = { NEE USA }
					}
				}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Riots throughout New England
	id = newengland.81
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.81"}
	title = newengland.81.t
	desc = newengland.81.d

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
			days > 30
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			has_state_flag = CAN_in_rebellion
			is_controlled_by = CAN
			OR = {
				state = 357 #Maine
				state = 934 #New Hampshire
				state = 933 #Vermont
				state = 932 #Massachusetts
				state = 935 #Rhode Island
				state = 931 #Connecticut
				state = 796 #Upstate New York
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 150
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_yankee_riots
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
				days > 50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
				days > 70
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.81.a
		clr_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		set_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		set_country_flag = CAN_yankee_riots
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
}

### Rejoining the ACW Winner
country_event = { # New England receives request
	id = newengland.90
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.90"}
	title = newengland.90.t

	desc = {
		text = newengland.90.d.forced
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = NEE_legitimacy
				value = NEE_threshold
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.90.d.choice
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = NEE_legitimacy
				value = NEE_threshold
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = requester
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_elected_government = yes
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = NEE_threshold
				value = 40
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_threshold
					value = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.90.a #It seems we have no choice...
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_neighbor_of = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = newengland.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.93
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.90.b #We should reunite
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = NEE_legitimacy
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = NEE_legitimacy
					value = 80
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_neighbor_of = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = newengland.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.93
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.90.c #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					has_elected_government = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.99
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England peacefully reuniting
	id = newengland.93
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.93"}
	title = newengland.93.t
	desc = newengland.93.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = NEE
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CAN
			has_war_with = NEE
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.93.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NEE = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			NEE = {
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = NEE
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = NEE
					}
					remove_claim_by = NEE
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = NEE
					}
					remove_core_of = NEE
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_nee_disobeyed
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				clr_country_flag = CAN_nee_disobeyed
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.100
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

			}

						is_core_of = NEE
					}
					remove_core_of = NEE
				}
			}
		}

					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			set_state_flag = CAN_in_rebellion
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = NEE
					}
					remove_claim_by = NEE
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = NEE
					}
					remove_core_of = NEE
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:requester = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.99
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England refused to join
	id = newengland.99
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.99"}
	title = newengland.99.t

	desc = {
		text = newengland.99.d.exists
		trigger = {
			country_exists = NEE
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.99.d.notexists
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = NEE
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				any_owned_state = {
					region = 186
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = NEE
				}
				NEE = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAN = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
					OR = {
						state = 357 #Maine
						state = 934 #New Hampshire
						state = 933 #Vermont
						state = 932 #Massachusetts
						state = 935 #Rhode Island
						state = 931 #Connecticut
						state = 796 #Upstate New York
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.99.a #Then it's war!
		trigger = {
			event_target:war_country = {
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_elected_government = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:war_country = {
					tag = CAN
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				set_country_flag = ACW_new_england_war@ROOT
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.99.b #We'll deal with this later
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			modifier = ITA_outraged
		}
	}
}

		name = newengland.183.a

		COR = {
		exists = yes
		has_war = no
		}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		COR = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
				}
			}
		}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = { tag = COR
		NEE = {
		exists = yes
		has_war = no
		}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		COR = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
				}
			}
		}
		}
	}
	option = {  ###Finish Them###
		name = newengland.183.b
		if = {
		limit = { tag = NEE}
		declare_war_on = {
		target = COR
		type = annex_everything
		}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = { tag = COR }
		declare_war_on = {
		target = NEE
		type = annex_everything
		}
		}
	}
}

            }
		}

				days = 5
			}
		}

	desc = newengland.243.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_UFO_4

	is_triggered_only = yes

		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = newengland.243.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = csa.128.t
			bonus = 2
			uses = 2
			category = nuclear
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = csa.128.t
			bonus = 5
			uses = 5
			category = computing_tech
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = csa.127.t
			bonus = 2
			uses = 2
			category = rocketry
			category = jet_technology
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# Appease the Elites
	id = newengland.264
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.264"}
	title = newengland.264.t
	desc = newengland.264.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Kennedy
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_KENNEDY_APPEASED
		}
		has_government = paternal_autocrat
		has_country_flag = NEE_plot_begin
	}
	
	
	option = { #Of Course
		name = newengland.264.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_WASHINGTON_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_KENNEDY_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_ASTOR_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_MILITARY_COUP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 20
	}
	option = { #Nah Fam
		name = newengland.264.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NEE_start_path
					option = NEE_CAN_MONARCHY
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NEE_pissed_off_nobles
	}
}

country_event = {# Monarchists Gain Control
	id = newengland.265
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.265"}
	title = newengland.265.t
	desc = newengland.265.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_washinton
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
   is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #no
		name = newengland.265.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NEE_start_path
					option = NEE_MILITARY_COUP
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = NEE_military_coup } }
			complete_national_focus = NEE_military_coup
		}
		set_country_flag = NEE_MILITARY_IN_POWER
	}
	
	option = { #yes
		name = newengland.265.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_WASHINGTON_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_KENNEDY_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_ASTOR_MONARCHY
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = NEE_MILITARY_IN_POWER
		create_country_leader = {# Joseph William Martin Jr.
			name = "New England Regency Council"
			desc = "POLITICS_BOSTON_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_NEE_Boston_Committee.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			traits = {}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = "New England Regency Council"
			long_name = "New England Regency Council"
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
		}
		add_ideas = NEE_republican_resistance
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.266
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

			}

				add_idea = NEE_elective_monarchy_idea
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #nah fuck that noise
		name = newengland.284.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}
